name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr

info:Stayed in April 2024

info:1 Review

posted:Posted April 6, 2024
msg:This business trip, I chose Jingxiang Hotel to stay. The accommodation experience is really good. The hotel has a large parking lot, which is an underground parking lot and a ground parking lot. The ground parking lot is also equipped with new energy charging piles. Parking is not only convenient but also convenient for guests to charge their cars. The hotel is located on Jiangfeng Road, Guyi Town, Sanjiang. It is a light luxury hotel with Dongzhai style. The hotel lobby is spacious and bright. The hotel front desk is very user-friendly. The waiter is enthusiastic and very attentive to check us in. He also introduced us to the overall environment of the hotel and the time and place for dinner and breakfast. The roof of the hotel is the breakfast restaurant and dinner area. You can see the beautiful scenery of Sanjiang County on the roof, especially the night view looks more beautiful. The hotel room facilities are complete, the network is unobstructed, the room hygiene is very clean, the items are neatly placed, the bathroom is separated into dry and wet, the room soundproofing is good, the bed sheets and quilts are neat and white, and the TV has many TV channels. The hotel is also equipped with a self-service laundry room and a gym, which is very convenient for guests. The hotel is also equipped with a children's playground and a mirror-like water lake, and the surrounding environment is particularly beautiful. It is worth recommending overall.

msg:Sanjiang Jingxiang Hotel can upgrade the room type if you book a member on Ctrip. The room is very large, about 40 square meters, with a small balcony, and you can see the Dongtian Palace Scenic Area opposite. The Dongtian Palace Scenic Area requires tickets, but basically few people visit. There is a museum next to the scenic area that is worth visiting. It is not convenient to eat around, but the hotel has a set meal on the 12th floor, with both Chinese and Western food. If the weather is good, you can eat on the terrace and see the night view of Sanjiang Fengyu Bridge. The hotel can buy a buffet breakfast. It is quite rich. The hotel has an underground parking lot, and free parking is very convenient. You can go in and out many times during your stay in the hotel. My family is satisfied with the stay.

name:f‚Äça‚Äçn‚Äçw‚Äço
info:Boutique Room (2 beds)
info:Stayed in November 2023
info:Family
info:8 Reviews
rating:4.7
posted:Posted November 17, 2023
msg:I stayed at Guilin Jingxiang Hotel first and thought it was good. So I went to Sanjiang and booked the same series. Advantages: The room is very large and comfortable. There are three chairs, enough to sit. The bathroom is also very large and can be turned around. There is also a special clothes hanger. It is very convenient to wash clothes. There is a public laundry room on the second floor. A bag of washing powder costs one yuan, which is very friendly to tourists who go there in summer. The bed is also very comfortable, with moderate hardness. The breakfast is rich, especially on weekends, with freshly ground coffee and several meat dishes, and the rice noodles are also very good. There are both Chinese and Western food, with rich varieties. For the level of 38 yuan, it is impeccable. The hotel also has lunch and dinner, which is convenient, inexpensive, and tastes good. The location should be said to be OK, opposite the Dong Nationality Museum, and the lights at night are very beautiful. Disadvantages: The hotel is at the high point of Jiangfeng Road. It is downhill when going out and uphill when coming back. It is very strenuous for us old people. There are no shops around. If we want to eat, we have to eat in the hotel, otherwise we have to eat takeout. We take a taxi every day. Fortunately, the starting price of a taxi in Sanjiang is only 5 yuan, which is really cheap. It costs 46 yuan to get to Chengyang Bazhai. The shower head in the room cannot be fixed. We are too lazy to call for maintenance, so we just make do. I hope that the room facilities can be checked frequently. In addition, the room is large, and the lighting seems a bit dim, especially there is no light above the shelf where the luggage is placed, which is inconvenient. Several lights in the room are not on. I don‚Äôt know if it is broken or to save electricity. Drinking water is said to be free, but in fact it is free for 4 bottles. If it exceeds 4 bottles, it will be charged. Every time we ask for water, we always have to pay a few yuan. Although it is not much money, I always feel uncomfortable. It is recommended to state it in the hotel introduction so that travelers can be mentally prepared. Overall, it is good and worth staying.
